{ meal.id = index; }); renderMeals(); } } // Add dish to meal function addDish(mealIndex) { appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.push({ name: '', mass: 0, calories: 0 }); renderMeals(); } // Remove dish from meal function removeDish(mealIndex, dishIndex) { if (appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.length &amp;amp;amp;gt; 1) { appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.splice(dishIndex, 1); renderMeals(); } } // Update dish data function updateDish(mealIndex, dishIndex, field, value) { appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes[dishIndex][field] = value; calculateMealStats(mealIndex); } // Calculate meal statistics function calculateMealStats(mealIndex) { const meal = appData.meals[mealIndex]; let totalMass = 0; let totalCalories = 0; meal.dishes.forEach(dish =&amp;amp;amp;gt; { totalMass += parseFloat(dish.mass) || 0; totalCalories += parseFloat(dish.calories) || 0; }); const density = totalMass &amp;amp;amp;gt; 0 ? (totalCalories / totalMass).toFixed(2) : 0; // Update display document.getElementById(`meal-mass-${mealIndex}`).textContent = totalMass.toFixed(1); document.getElementById(`meal-calories-${mealIndex}`).textContent = totalCalories.toFixed(0); document.getElementById(`meal-density-${mealIndex}`).textContent = density; } // Render all meals function renderMeals() { const container = document.getElementById('mealsContainer'); container.innerHTML = ''; appData.meals.forEach((meal, mealIndex) =&amp;amp;amp;gt; { const mealDiv = document.createElement('div'); mealDiv.className = 'meal-section'; mealDiv.innerHTML = ` &amp;amp;amp;lt;div class="meal-header"&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;h3&amp;amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;amp;lt;span class="emoji"&amp;amp;amp;gt;üçΩÔ∏è&amp;amp;amp;lt;/span&amp;amp;amp;gt;–ü—Ä–∏—ë–º –ø–∏—â–∏ ${mealIndex + 1}&amp;amp;amp;lt;/h3&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;button class="btn btn--secondary btn--sm" onclick="removeMeal(${mealIndex})" ${appData.meals.length &amp;amp;amp;lt;= 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}&amp;amp;amp;gt; üóëÔ∏è –£–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å &amp;amp;amp;lt;/button&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;/div&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;div id="dishes-${mealIndex}"&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;!-- Dishes will be rendered here --&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;span id="meal-mass-${mealIndex}"&amp;amp;amp;gt;0.0&amp;amp;amp;lt;/span&amp;amp;amp;gt; –≥&amp;amp;amp;lt;/div&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;div&amp;amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;amp;gt;–û–±—â–∏–µ –∫–∞–ª–æ—Ä–∏–∏:&amp;amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;span id="meal-calories-${mealIndex}"&amp;amp;amp;gt;0&amp;amp;amp;lt;/span&amp;amp;amp;gt; –∫–∫–∞–ª&amp;amp;amp;lt;/div&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;div&amp;amp;amp;gt;&amp;amp;amp;lt;strong&amp;amp;amp;gt;–ü–ª–æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫–∞–ª–æ—Ä–∏–π:&amp;amp;amp;lt;/strong&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;span id="meal-density-${mealIndex}"&amp;amp;amp;gt;0.00&amp;amp;amp;lt;/span&amp;amp;amp;gt; –∫–∫–∞–ª/–≥&amp;amp;amp;lt;/div&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;/div&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;div class="add-buttons"&amp;amp;amp;gt; `; container.appendChild(mealDiv); renderDishes(mealIndex); calculateMealStats(mealIndex); }); updateCodeDisplay(); } // Render dishes for a specific meal function renderDishes(mealIndex) { const dishesContainer = document.getElementById(`dishes-${mealIndex}`); dishesContainer.innerHTML = ''; appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.forEach((dish, dishIndex) =&amp;amp;amp;gt; { const dishDiv = document.createElement('div'); dishDiv.className = 'dish-grid'; dishDiv.innerHTML = ` &amp;amp;amp;lt;div class="form-group"&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;label class="form-label"&amp;amp;amp;gt;üçõ –ù–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –±–ª—é–¥–∞&amp;amp;amp;lt;/label&amp;amp;amp;gt; &amp;amp;amp;lt;input type="text" class="form-control" value="${dish.name}" placeholder="–ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä: –ö—É—Ä–∏–Ω–∞—è –≥—Ä—É–¥–∫–∞" onchange="updateDish(${mealIndex}, ${dishIndex}, 'name', this.value)"&amp;amp;amp;gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;script&gt; // Global data storage let appData = { meals: [] }; // Initialize app function initApp() { // Set today's date document.getElementById('data').value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]; // Create initial 6 meals for (let i = 0; i &lt; 6; i++) { addMeal(); } updateCodeDisplay(); // Add event listeners for parameters that trigger calculations document.getElementById('data').addEventListener('change', calculateDayOfProgram); } // Calculate day of program based on start date (assuming program started 30 days ago) function calculateDayOfProgram() { const currentDate = new Date(document.getElementById('data').value); const startDate = new Date(); startDate.setDate(startDate.getDate() - 30); // Assume program started 30 days ago const diffTime = Math.abs(currentDate - startDate); const diffDays = Math.ceil(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)); document.getElementById('denProgrammy').value = diffDays; } // Add a new meal function addMeal() { const mealIndex = appData.meals.length; const meal = { id: mealIndex, dishes: [] }; // Add 6 initial dishes for (let i = 0; i &lt; 6; i++) { meal.dishes.push({ name: '', mass: 0, calories: 0 }); } appData.meals.push(meal); renderMeals(); } // Remove a meal function removeMeal(mealIndex) { if (appData.meals.length &gt; 1) { appData.meals.splice(mealIndex, 1); // Reindex meals appData.meals.forEach((meal, index) =&gt; { meal.id = index; }); renderMeals(); } } // Add dish to meal function addDish(mealIndex) { appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.push({ name: '', mass: 0, calories: 0 }); renderMeals(); } // Remove dish from meal function removeDish(mealIndex, dishIndex) { if (appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.length &gt; 1) { appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.splice(dishIndex, 1); renderMeals(); } } // Update dish data function updateDish(mealIndex, dishIndex, field, value) { appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes[dishIndex][field] = value; calculateMealStats(mealIndex); } // Calculate meal statistics function calculateMealStats(mealIndex) { const meal = appData.meals[mealIndex]; let totalMass = 0; let totalCalories = 0; meal.dishes.forEach(dish =&gt; { totalMass += parseFloat(dish.mass) || 0; totalCalories += parseFloat(dish.calories) || 0; }); const density = totalMass &gt; 0 ? (totalCalories / totalMass).toFixed(2) : 0; // Update display document.getElementById(`meal-mass-${mealIndex}`).textContent = totalMass.toFixed(1); document.getElementById(`meal-calories-${mealIndex}`).textContent = totalCalories.toFixed(0); document.getElementById(`meal-density-${mealIndex}`).textContent = density; } // Render all meals function renderMeals() { const container = document.getElementById('mealsContainer'); container.innerHTML = ''; appData.meals.forEach((meal, mealIndex) =&gt; { const mealDiv = document.createElement('div'); mealDiv.className = 'meal-section'; mealDiv.innerHTML = ` &lt;div class="meal-header"&gt; &lt;h3&gt;&lt;span class="emoji"&gt;üçΩÔ∏è&lt;/span&gt;–ü—Ä–∏—ë–º –ø–∏—â–∏ ${mealIndex + 1}&lt;/h3&gt; &lt;button class="btn btn--secondary btn--sm" onclick="removeMeal(${mealIndex})" ${appData.meals.length &lt;= 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}&gt; üóëÔ∏è –£–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å &lt;/button&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div id="dishes-${mealIndex}"&gt; &lt;!-- Dishes will be rendered here --&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class="meal-stats"&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;strong&gt;–û–±—â–∞—è –º–∞—Å—Å–∞:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;span id="meal-mass-${mealIndex}"&gt;0.0&lt;/span&gt; –≥&lt;/div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;strong&gt;–û–±—â–∏–µ –∫–∞–ª–æ—Ä–∏–∏:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;span id="meal-calories-${mealIndex}"&gt;0&lt;/span&gt; –∫–∫–∞–ª&lt;/div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;strong&gt;–ü–ª–æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫–∞–ª–æ—Ä–∏–π:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;span id="meal-density-${mealIndex}"&gt;0.00&lt;/span&gt; –∫–∫–∞–ª/–≥&lt;/div&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class="add-buttons"&gt; &lt;button class="btn btn--secondary btn--sm" onclick="addDish(${mealIndex})"&gt; ‚ûï –î–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –±–ª—é–¥–æ &lt;/button&gt; &lt;/div&gt; `; container.appendChild(mealDiv); renderDishes(mealIndex); calculateMealStats(mealIndex); }); updateCodeDisplay(); } // Render dishes for a specific meal function renderDishes(mealIndex) { const dishesContainer = document.getElementById(`dishes-${mealIndex}`); dishesContainer.innerHTML = ''; appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.forEach((dish, dishIndex) =&gt; { const dishDiv = document.createElement('div'); dishDiv.className = 'dish-grid'; dishDiv.innerHTML = ` &lt;div class="form-group"&gt; &lt;label class="form-label"&gt;üçõ –ù–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –±–ª—é–¥–∞&lt;/label&gt; &lt;input type="text" class="form-control" value="${dish.name}" placeholder="–ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä: –ö—É—Ä–∏–Ω–∞—è –≥—Ä—É–¥–∫–∞" onchange="updateDish(${mealIndex}, ${dishIndex}, 'name', this.value)"&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class="form-group"&gt; &lt;label class="form-label"&gt;‚öñÔ∏è –ú–∞—Å—Å–∞ (–≥)&lt;/label&gt; &lt;input type="number" class="form-control" value="${dish.mass || ''}" step="0.1" placeholder="0.0" onchange="updateDish(${mealIndex}, ${dishIndex}, 'mass', this.value)"&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class="form-group"&gt; &lt;label class="form-label"&gt;üî• –ö–∞–ª–æ—Ä–∏–∏ (–∫–∫–∞–ª)&lt;/label&gt; &lt;input type="number" class="form-control" value="${dish.calories || ''}" step="1" placeholder="0" onchange="updateDish(${mealIndex}, ${dishIndex}, 'calories', this.value)"&gt; &lt;/div&gt; &lt;div&gt; &lt;button class="remove-dish" onclick="removeDish(${mealIndex}, ${dishIndex})" ${appData.meals[mealIndex].dishes.length &lt;= 1 ? 'disabled' : ''} title="–£–¥–∞–ª–∏—Ç—å –±–ª—é–¥–æ"&gt; ‚úñ &lt;/button&gt; &lt;/div&gt; `; dishesContainer.appendChild(dishDiv); }); } // Update code display function updateCodeDisplay() { setTimeout(() =&gt;
